<text>Okay.  I am a huge fan of Cold Stone.  They have really good ice cream and it is 10x better than everyone else.  So, on pure taste alone they would get five stars.  Having said that I do have two grips.  First, this location has been under staffed the last five times I have been here and the one guy they do have is super slow. The last time I was in line for twenty minutes with three people ahead of me and just gave up. Second, the prices are really high. Be prepared to spend over $6. I may seem like I am nitpicking but at least I have stated what I like and dislike about this place.  In the future I will go to Cold Stone but try to find another location that is quicker. I was in Death Valley in June, 1970.  It was 124 degrees.  We had to keep the heat on in the car to try to vent and cool the engine.  Stick your head out the window of the moving car... it felt like a hair dryer blowing in your face on high, close up.  Anyone who stays in this location to sell gas to travelers... deserves a bonus/premium on the gas price!  If they are open... and selling gas... service is excellent... < Review>
I've known the owner and artist Jason Dunn when I first got ink from him 8 years ago. I followed his work ever since. His skills and work has greatly improved since then and his positive vibes still hasn't changed.
He and his team puts guest experience, service, and safety as the top priority for their business and trade. < Text>
Got a tattoo done yesterday at Tattoo Alchemy. My artist was Art (with some help from Jason).

My tattoo was pretty straight forward - got my fiancee's name on my chest. Art drew out his design and with a couple of tweaks, found one that i was happy with.

I was a bit anxious at first, with the first few times the needle hit my skin I wondered if i made the right decision. At this point Jason did a few lines (Jason said he has been working with Art on tattooing/techniques). After Jason did his lines and gave Art a couple of tips, it was smooth sailing from there. Art did a great job - he delivered.

The process took a little longer than expected, but that was OK by me. Art had Jason check his work about 2-3 times before we finished. Jason gave Art pointers and making sure all the line work matched up so the lettering didn't seem like they were all separate tattoos.

At the end, Art and Jason both explained the after care procedure for the tattoo. Would definitely go back for more -- with Art or any artist there (you can tell they take care of their customers - Art, Jason, all the artists i saw there, they don't want to give you a good tattoo -- they want to give you a PERFECT tattoo... Jason "signed off" on the tattoo Art gave me. If MY tattoo is good enough for an Ink Master Champion, it's good enough for me.<//Text>

< text>
I got their wings lunch combo with the Teri Wings, a side of kimchi, and a can of soda. I had to add a side of pickled radish to get it up to the $10 minimum for cards. The wings tasted really delicious, though I was hoping for a little more sauce (but that could just be me, I love slathering everything in sauce). You also get a pretty large amount for the sides so I think the price was worth it. I'll definitely be going back to try out some of their other flavors of wings. There isn't that much seating, but the place was empty when I went during lunch time, and my food was prepared really quickly. I'd definitely recommend this place if you haven't tried it!<//text>
